If it is not specified, it defaults to an empty selector.\n68: \t// +optional\n69: \tPodSelector metav1.LabelSelector `json:\"podSelector\" protobuf:\"bytes,1,opt,name=podSelector\"`\n70: \n71: \t// ingress is a list of ingress rules to be applied to the selected pods.\n72: \t// Traffic is allowed to a pod if there are no NetworkPolicies selecting the pod\n73: \t// (and cluster policy otherwise allows the traffic), OR if the traffic source is\n74: \t// the pod's local node, OR if the traffic matches at least one ingress rule\n75: \t// across all of the NetworkPolicy objects whose podSelector matches the pod. If\n76: \t// this field is empty then this NetworkPolicy does not allow any traffic (and serves\n77: \t// solely to ensure that the pods it selects are isolated by default)\n78: \t// +optional\n79: \t// +listType=atomic\n80: \t// +k8s:alpha(since: \"1.36\")=+k8s:optional\n81: \tIngress []NetworkPolicyIngressRule `json:\"ingress,omitempty\" protobuf:\"bytes,2,rep,name=ingress\"`\n82: \n83: \t// egress is a list of egress rules to be applied to the selected pods. Outgoing traffic\n84: \t// is allowed if there are no NetworkPolicies selecting the pod (and cluster policy\n85: \t// otherwise allows the traffic), OR if the traffic matches at least one egress rule\n86: \t// across all of the NetworkPolicy objects whose podSelector matches the pod. If\n87: \t// this field is empty then this NetworkPolicy limits all outgoing traffic (and serves\n88: \t// solely to ensure that the pods it selects are isolated by default).\n89: \t// This field is beta-level in 1.8\n90: \t// +optional\n91: \t// +listType=atomic\n92: \t// +k8s:alpha(since: \"1.36\")=+k8s:optional\n93: \tEgress []NetworkPolicyEgressRule `json:\"egress,omitempty\" protobuf:\"bytes,3,rep,name=egress\"`\n94: \n95: \t// policyTypes is a list of rule types that the NetworkPolicy relates to.\n96: \t// Valid options are [\"Ingress\"], [\"Egress\"], or [\"Ingress\", \"Egress\"].\n97: \t// If this field is not specified, it will default based on the existence of ingress or egress rules;\n98: \t// policies that contain an egress section are assumed to affect egress, and all policies\n99: \t// (whether or not they contain an ingress section) are assumed to affect ingress.\n100: \t// If you want to write an egress-only policy, you must explicitly specify policyTypes [ \"Egress\" ].\n101: \t// Likewise, if you want to write a policy that specifies that no egress is allowed,\n102: \t// you must specify a policyTypes value that include \"Egress\" (since such a policy would not include\n103: \t// an egress section and would otherwise default to just [ \"Ingress\" ]).\n104: \t// This field is beta-level in 1.8\n105: \t// +optional\n106: \t// +listType=atomic\n107: \tPolicyTypes []PolicyType `json:\"policyTypes,omitempty\" protobuf:\"bytes,4,rep,name=policyTypes,casttype=PolicyType\"`\n108: }\n109: \n110: // NetworkPolicyIngressRule describes a particular set of traffic that is allowed to the pods\n111: // matched by a NetworkPolicySpec's podSelector. The traffic must match both ports and from.\n112: type NetworkPolicyIngressRule struct {\n113: \t// ports is a list of ports which should be made accessible on the pods selected for\n114: \t// this rule. Each item in this list is combined using a logical OR. If this field is\n115: \t// empty or missing, this rule matches all ports (traffic not restricted by port).\n116: \t// If this field is present and contains at least one item, then this rule allows\n117: \t// traffic only if the traffic matches at least one port in the list.\n118: \t// +optional\n119: \t// +listType=atomic\n120: \tPorts []NetworkPolicyPort `json:\"ports,omitempty\" protobuf:\"bytes,1,rep,name=ports\"`\n121: \n122: \t// from is a list of sources which should be able to access the pods selected for this rule.\n123: \t// Items in this list are combined using a logical OR operation. If this field is\n124: \t// empty or missing, this rule matches all sources (traffic not restricted by\n125: \t// source). If this field is present and contains at least one item, this rule\n126: \t// allows traffic only if the traffic matches at least one item in the from list.\n127: \t// +optional\n128: \t// +listType=atomic\n129: \t// +k8s:alpha(since: \"1.36\")=+k8s:optional\n130: \tFrom []NetworkPolicyPeer `json:\"from,omitempty\" protobuf:\"bytes,2,rep,name=from\"`\n131: }\n132: \n133: // NetworkPolicyEgressRule describes a particular set of traffic that is allowed out of pods\n134: // matched by a NetworkPolicySpec's podSelector. Currently it can\\n488: \\t// contain characters disallowed from the conventional \\\"path\\\" part of a URL\\n489: \\t// as defined by RFC 3986. Matching is\\n498: \\t//   done on a path element by element basis. A path element refers is the\\n499: \\t//   list of labels in the path split by the '/' separator.
